import os,re,collections

root="."
imports=collections.defaultdict(set)
reverse=collections.defaultdict(set)
entrypoints=set()

for dp,_,fs in os.walk(root):
    for f in fs:
        if f.endswith(".py"):
            p=os.path.join(dp,f)
            try:
                txt=open(p,errors="ignore").read()
            except: continue

            # imports
            for m in re.findall(r'^\s*(?:from\s+([\w\.]+)|import\s+([\w\.]+))',txt,re.M):
                mod=(m[0] or m[1]).split('.')[0]
                imports[p].add(mod)

            # entrypoints
            if "__main__" in txt or re.search(r'\bmain\s*\(',txt):
                entrypoints.add(p)

# reverse graph
for f,mods in imports.items():
PY  print(f"{c:4d}  {m}")common(15):ods in imports.values() for m in mods)
